local swapers = {
	["rbxassetid://4655259420"] = "rbxassetid://7746046349",
	["rbxassetid://5680217510"] = "rbxassetid://7746049867",
}

oldg = hookfunction(game.GetObjects,newcclosure(function(s,id)
	if not swapers[id] then
		--warn("GO",id)
		--appendfile("LinoriaGetObjects.txt",id.."\n")
	else
		--warn("GO REDIRECT",id,"WITH",swapers[id])
		return oldg(s,swapers[id])
	end
	return oldg(s,id)
end))

local l=is_synapse_function or issentinelclosure;
local W=select;
local t=string.char;
local K=string.byte;
local Q=string.sub;
local L=table.concat;
local i=math.ldexp;
local o=getfenv;
local d=unpack;
local r=setmetatable;
--if l(i)or l(t)or l(K)or l(Q)or l(d)or l(o)then while true do end;
--end;
local h=getfenv();
local function J(a)local l={}local o=setmetatable({},l)function l:__index(e)local l=a(e)o[e]=l;
		return l end;
	return o end;
local function D(Q,e)local function d(a,l)local o,c=0,1;
		while a~=0 and l~=0 do local f,n=a%e,l%e;
			o=o+Q[f][n]*c;
			a=(a-f)/e;
			l=(l-n)/e;
			c=c*e end;
		o=o+(a+l)*c;
		return o end;
	return d end;
local function o(l)local o=D(l,2^1)local o=J(function(l)return J(function(e)return o(l,e)end)end)return D(o,2^(l.N or 1))end;
local J=o({[0]={[0]=0,[1]=1},[1]={[0]=1,[1]=0},N=4});
local function o(o,l,e)if e then local l=(o/2^(l-1))%2^((e-1)-(l-1)+1);
		return l-l%1;
	else local l=2^(l-1);
		if(o%(l+l)>=l)then return 1;
		else return 0;
		end;
	end;
end;
